# Drevlians
country_event = {
	id = et.100
	title = "et.EVTNAME100"
	desc = "et.EVTDESC100"
	picture = CITY_DEVELOPMENT_eventPicture

	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		owns = 1943
		is_year = 2598
		OR = {
			1941 = { is_empty = yes }
			4115 = { is_empty = yes }
		}
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 240
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "et.EVTOPTA100"
		if = {
			limit = { 1941 = { is_empty = yes } }
			1941 = { 
				cede_province = DRV 
				add_core = DRV
				change_trade_goods = wool
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { 4115 = { is_empty = yes } }
			4115 = { 
				cede_province = DRV 
				add_core = DRV
				change_trade_goods = wool
			}
		}
                if = {
			limit = { 12891 = { is_empty = yes } }
			12891 = { 
				cede_province = DRV 
				add_core = DRV
				change_trade_goods = wool
			}
		}
                if = {
			limit = { 12892 = { is_empty = yes } }
			12892 = { 
				cede_province = DRV 
				add_core = DRV
				change_trade_goods = wool
			}
		}
                if = {
			limit = { 12893 = { is_empty = yes } }
			12893 = { 
				cede_province = DRV 
				add_core = DRV
				change_trade_goods = wool
			}
		}
                if = {
			limit = { 12894 = { is_empty = yes } }
			12894 = { 
				cede_province = DRV 
				add_core = DRV
				change_trade_goods = wool
			}
		}
                if = {
			limit = { 12895 = { is_empty = yes } }
			12895 = { 
				cede_province = DRV 
				add_core = DRV
				change_trade_goods = wool
			}
		}
                if = {
			limit = { 12896 = { is_empty = yes } }
			12896 = { 
				cede_province = DRV 
				add_core = DRV
				change_trade_goods = wool
			}
		}
                if = {
			limit = { 12897 = { is_empty = yes } }
			12897 = { 
				cede_province = DRV 
				add_core = DRV
				change_trade_goods = wool
			}
		}
                if = {
			limit = { 12898 = { is_empty = yes } }
			12898 = { 
				cede_province = DRV

                if = {
			limit = { 12899 = { is_empty = yes } }
			12899 = { 
				cede_province = DRV 
				add_core = DRV
				change_trade_goods = wool
			}
		}
                if = {

			12900 = { 
				cede_province = DRV

				change_trade_goods = wool

# Lendians
country_event = {
	id = et.102
	title = "et.EVTNAME100"
	desc = "et.EVTDESC100"
	picture = CITY_DEVELOPMENT_eventPicture

	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		owns = 279
		is_year = 2598
		OR = {
			277 = { is_empty = yes }
			278 = { is_empty = yes }
		}
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 240
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "et.EVTOPTA100"
		if = {
			limit = { 277 = { is_empty = yes } }
			277 = { 
				cede_province = LDN
				add_core = LDN
				change_trade_goods = wool
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { 278 = { is_empty = yes } }
			278 = { 
				cede_province = LDN
				add_core = LDN
				change_trade_goods = wool
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { 4537 = { is_empty = yes } }
			4537 = { 
				cede_province = LDN
				add_core = LDN
				change_trade_goods = wool
			}
		}

			limit = { 12879 = { is_empty = yes } }

			limit = { 12880 = { is_empty = yes } }
			12880 = {

			limit = { 12881 = { is_empty = yes } }
			12881 = {

			}
		}
                if = {
			limit = { 12882 = { is_empty = yes } }
			12882 = { 
				cede_province = LDN
				add_core = LDN
				change_trade_goods = wool
			}
		}
                if = {
			limit = { 12883 = { is_empty = yes } }
			12883 = { 
				cede_province = LDN
				add_core = LDN
				change_trade_goods = wool
			}
		}
                if = {
			limit = { 12884 = { is_empty = yes } }
			12884 = { 
				cede_province = LDN
				add_core = LDN
				change_trade_goods = wool
			}

                if = {
			limit = { 12888 = { is_empty = yes } }

			}
		}
		279 = {
			change_culture = ruthenian
			add_core = LDN
			nationalist_rebels = 2
		}
		1940 = {
			change_culture = ruthenian
			add_core = LDN
			nationalist_rebels = 2
		}
		LDN = { every_neighbor_country = { add_truce_with = LDN } }
	}
}

# Curonians

	id = et.103
	title = "et.EVTNAME100"
	desc = "et.EVTDESC100"
	picture = CITY_DEVELOPMENT_eventPicture

	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		owns = 41
		is_year = 2598
		OR = {
			40 = { is_empty = yes }
			39 = { is_empty = yes }
			1935 = { is_empty = yes }
		}
	}

		months = 240

# Mombasa, Malindi and Pate
country_event = {
	id = et.139
	title = "et.EVTNAME101"
	desc = "et.EVTDESC101"
	picture = SHIP_SAILING_eventPicture

	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		owns = 1205
		is_year = 2948
		1202 = { is_empty = yes }
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 120
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "et.EVTOPTA101"
		1202 = { 
			cede_province = MBA
			add_core = MBA
			change_trade_goods = ivory
			change_religion = sunni
		}
		if = {
			limit = { 1200 = { is_empty = yes } }
			1200 = { 
				cede_province = MBA
				add_core = MBA
				change_trade_goods = ivory
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { 1203 = { is_empty = yes } }
			1203 = { 
				cede_province = MLI
				add_core = MLI
				change_trade_goods = ivory
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { 1204 = { is_empty = yes } }
			1204 = { 
				cede_province = MLI
				add_core = MLI
				change_trade_goods = ivory
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { 2796 = { is_empty = yes } }
			2796 = { 
				cede_province = PTE
				add_core = PTE
				change_trade_goods = cloth
			}
		}
                if = {
			limit = { 10964 = { is_empty = yes } }
			10964 = { 
				cede_province = MLI
				add_core = MLI
				change_trade_goods = ivory
			}
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					technology_group = indian
					technology_group = muslim
					technology_group = ottoman
					technology_group = east_african
				}
			}
			discover_province = 1200
			discover_province = 1202
			discover_province = 1203
			discover_province = 1448
		}
		MBA = { every_neighbor_country = { add_truce_with = MBA } }
		MLI = { every_neighbor_country = { add_truce_with = MLI } }
		PTE = { every_neighbor_country = { add_truce_with = PTE } }
	}
}

	desc = "et.EVTDESC100"

	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		owns = 662
		is_year = 2598
		OR = {
			661 = { is_empty = yes }

		}
	}

		months = 480
	}
